END, [p.ProductTags].[TagId]
FROM [ProductTags] AS [p.ProductTags]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [p2].[DateCreated], [p2].[Id]
    FROM [Products] AS [p2]
    INNER JOIN [ProductCategories] AS [p.ProductCategory2] ON [p2].[CategoryId] = [p.ProductCategory2].[Id]
    ORDER BY [p2].[DateCreated] DESC, [p2].[Id]
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t2] ON [p.ProductTags].[ProductId] = [t2].[Id]
ORDER BY [t2].[DateCreated] DESC, [t2].[Id]" (0723d8ff)
